Multiple targeted search queries to maximize information gathering\n    search_queries = [\n        \'"Embroidery from Uzbekistan" 2008 painting artist\',\n        \'"Embroidery from Uzbekistan" 2008 artwork fruits depicted\',\n        \'Uzbekistan embroidery painting 2008 museum collection\',\n        \'"Embroidery from Uzbekistan" artist 2008 auction gallery\',\n        \'Uzbekistan textile art painting 2008 fruits motifs\',\n        \'2008 painting "Embroidery from Uzbekistan" visual description\'\n    ]\n    \n    all_search_results = []\n    \n    for i, query in enumerate(search_queries):\n        print(f\'\\n=== SEARCH {i+1}/6: "{query}" ===\')\n        \n        params = {\n            "q": query,\n            "api_key": api_key,\n            "engine": "google",\n            "google_domain": "google.com",\n            "safe": "off",\n            "num": 10\n        }\n        \n        try:\n            response = requests.get("https://serpapi.com/search.json", params=params)\n            \n            if response.status_code == 200:\n                results = response.json()\n                \n                if results.get("organic_results"):\n                    print(f\'Found {len(results["organic_results"])} results\')\n                    \n                    for j, result in enumerate(results["organic_results"]):\n                        title = result.get(\'title\', \'No title\')\n                        link = result.get(\'link\', \'No link\')\n                        snippet = result.get(\'snippet\', \'No snippet\')\n                        \n                        print(f\'\\n  Result {j+1}:\')\n                        print(f\'  Title: {title}\')\n                        print(f\'  URL: {link}\')\n                        print(f\'  Snippet: {snippet}\')\n                        \n                        # Check for key indicators\n                        combined_text = f\'{title} {snippet}\'.lower()\n                        \n                        key_findings = []\n                        if \'embroidery from uzbekistan\' in combined_text:\n                            key_findings.append(\'Exact title match\')\n                        if \'2008\' in combined_text:\n                            key_findings.append(\'Year 2008 mentioned\')\n                        if any(term in combined_text for term in [\'artist\', \'painter\', \'creator\']):\n                            key_findings.append(\'Artist information\')\n                        if any(term in combined_text for term in [\'fruit\', \'fruits\', \'motif\', \'pattern\']):\n                            key_findings.append(\'Fruit/motif content\')\n                        if any(term in combined_text for term in [\'museum\', \'gallery\', \'collection\', \'auction\']):\n                            key_findings.append(\'Institutional source\')\n                        if any(term in combined_text for term in [\'image\', \'photo\', \'visual\', \'picture\']):\n                            key_findings.append(\'Visual content available\')\n                        \n                        if key_findings:\n                            print(f\'  *** KEY FINDINGS: {key_findings} ***\')\n                        \n                        # Store result with metadata\n                        all_search_results.append({\n                            \'search_query\': query,\n                            \'search_index\': i+1,\n                            \'result_index\': j+1,\n                            \'title\': title,\n                            \'link\': link,\n                            \'snippet\': snippet,\n                            \'key_findings\': key_findings,\n                            \'relevance_score\': len(key_findings)\n                        })\n                        \n                        print(\'-\' * 60)\n                else:\n                    print(\'No organic results found for this query\')\n            else:\n                print(f\'Search failed with status: {response.status_code}\')\n                print(f\'Response: {response.text[:200]}...\')\n                \n        except Exception as e:\n            print(f\'Search error: {str(e)}\')\n        \n        # Rate limiting\n        time.sleep(1.5)\n    \n    # Save comprehensive search results\n    search_data = {\n        \'painting_title\': \'Embroidery from Uzbekistan\',\n        \'painting_year\': 2008,\n        \'search_timestamp\': datetime.now().isoformat(),\n        \'total_queries\': len(search_queries),\n        \'queries_used\': search_queries,\n        \'total_results\': len(all_search_results),\n        \'search_results\': all_search_results\n    }\n    \n    with open(\'workspace/embroidery_uzbekistan_2008_search_results.json\', \'w\') as f:\n        json.dump(search_data, f, indent=2, ensure_ascii=False)\n    \n    print(f\'\\n=== COMPREHENSIVE SEARCH RESULTS SUMMARY ===\')\n    print(f\'Total search queries executed: {len(search_queries)}\')\n    print(f\'Total results collected: {len(all_search_results)}\')\n    print(f\'Results saved to: workspace/embroidery_uzbekistan_2008_search_results.json\')\n    \n    # Analyze and prioritize results\n    high_relevance_results = [r for r in all_search_results if r[\'relevance_score\'] >= 2]\n    exact_title_matches = [r for r in all_search_results if \'Exact title match\' in r.get(\'key_findings\', [])]\n    artist_info_results = [r for r in all_search_results if \'Artist information\' in r.get(\'key_findings\', [])]\n    visual_content_results = [r for r in all_search_results if \'Visual content available\' in r.get(\'key_findings\', [])]\n    institutional_results = [r for r in all_search_results if \'Institutional source\' in r.get(\'key_findings\', [])]\n    \n    print(f\'\\n=== PRIORITY ANALYSIS ===\')\n    print(f\'High relevance results (2+ key findings): {len(high_relevance_results)}\')\n    print(f\'Exact title matches: {len(exact_title_matches)}\')\n    print(f\'Results with artist information: {len(artist_info_results)}\')\n    print(f\'Results with visual content: {len(visual_content_results)}\')\n    print(f\'Institutional sources: {len(institutional_results)}\')\n    \n    # Show top priority results\n    if exact_title_matches:\n        print(f\'\\nüéØ EXACT TITLE MATCHES FOUND:\')\n        for result in exact_title_matches[:3]:\n            print(f\'  ‚Ä¢ {result["title"]}\')  \n            print(f\'    URL: {result["link"]}\')\n            print(f\'    Findings: {result["key_findings"]}\')\n            print()\n    \n    if high_relevance_results:\n        print(f\'\\n‚≠ê TOP HIGH-RELEVANCE RESULTS:\')\n        # Sort by relevance score\n        sorted_results = sorted(high_relevance_results, key=lambda x: x[\'relevance_score\'], reverse=True)\n        for result in sorted_results[:5]:\n            print(f\'  ‚Ä¢ Score {result["relevance_score"]}: {result["title"]}\')\n            print(f\'    URL: {result["link"]}\')\n            print(f\'    Findings: {result["key_findings"]}\')\n            print()\n    \n    # Create priority analysis summary\n    priority_summary = {\n        \'analysis_timestamp\': datetime.now().isoformat(),\n        \'total_results_analyzed\': len(all_search_results),\n        \'priority_categories\': {\n            \'exact_title_matches\': len(exact_title_matches),\n            \'high_relevance_results\': len(high_relevance_results),\n            \'artist_information_available\': len(artist_info_results),\n            \'visual_content_available\': len(visual_content_results),\n            \'institutional_sources\': len(institutional_results)\n        },\n        \'top_exact_matches\': exact_title_matches[:3],\n        \'top_high_relevance\': sorted(high_relevance_results, key=lambda x: x[\'relevance_score\'], reverse=True)[:5] if high_relevance_results else [],\n        \'next_steps\': [\n            \'Analyze exact title matches for artist identification\',\n            \'Extract visual descriptions from high-relevance results\',\n            \'Cross-reference institutional sources for authenticity\',\n            \'Look for auction records or gallery exhibitions\'\n        ]\n    }\n    \n    with open(\'workspace/priority_analysis_embroidery_uzbekistan.json\', \'w\') as f:\n        json.dump(priority_summary, f, indent=2, ensure_ascii=False)\n    \n    print(f\'\\nPriority analysis saved to: workspace/priority_analysis_embroidery_uzbekistan.json\')\n    \nelse:\n    print(\'‚ùå No SERPAPI key available - cannot perform Google searches\')\n    print(\'Alternative approach: Direct web searches on art databases\')\n    \n    # Try direct searches on major art databases without API\n    art_database_urls = [\n        \'https://www.artnet.com/artists/\',\n        \'https://www.mutualart.com/Artist/\',\n        \'https://www.benezit.com/\',\n        \'https://www.worldcat.org/search?q=\'\n    ]\n    \n    print(\'\\nAttempting direct searches on art databases...\')\n    \n    headers = {\n        \'User-Agent\': \'Mozilla/5.0 (Windows NT 10.0; Win64; x64) AppleWebKit/537.36 (KHTML, like Gecko) Chrome/91.0.4472.124 Safari/537.36\'\n    }\n    \n    for i, base_url in enumerate(art_database_urls):\n        search_url = f\'{base_url}Embroidery+from+Uzbekistan+2008\'\n        print(f\'\\nTrying art database {i+1}: {search_url}\')\n        \n        try:\n            response = requests.get(search_url, headers=headers, timeout=15)\n            print(f\'Response status: {response.status_code}\')\n            \n            if response.status_code == 200:\n                filename = f\'workspace/art_database_search_{i+1}.html\'\n                with open(filename, \'w\', encoding=\'utf-8\') as f:\n                    f.write(response.text)\n                print(f\'Saved response to: {filename}\')\n            \n        except Exception as e:\n            print(f\'Error accessing {base_url}: {str(e)}\')\n        \n        time.sleep(2)\n\nprint(\'\\n=== INITIAL SEARCH PHASE COMPLETE ===\')\nprint(\'Next steps:\')\nprint(\'1. Analyze collected search results for exact matches\')\nprint(\'2. Extract artist information from promising sources\')\nprint(\'3. headers=headers, timeout=30)\n        print(f\'Response status: {response.status_code}\')\n        \n        if response.status_code == 200:\n            # Determine file type and save appropriately\n            if url.endswith(\'.pdf\'):\n                filename = f\'workspace/dayton_pdf_transcript_{i+1}.pdf\'\n                with open(filename, \'wb\') as f:\n                    f.write(response.content)\n                print(f\'‚úì PDF saved to: {filename}\')\n                print(f\'  File size: {len(response.content):,} bytes\')\n                \n                # Note: else:\n                # HTML content\n                filename = f\'workspace/dayton_source_{i+1}.html\'\n                with open(filename, \'w\', encoding=\'utf-8\') as f:\n                    f.write(response.text)\n                print(f\'‚úì HTML saved to: {filename}\')\n                print(f\'  Content length: {len(response.text):,} characters\')\n                \n                # \'grapes\', \'pear\', \'cherry\', \'peach\', \'plum\', \'banana\', \'lemon\', \'lime\']\n                found_fruits = []\n                \n                for keyword in fruit_keywords:\n                    if keyword in text_content:\n                        found_fruits.append(keyword)\n                \n                if found_fruits:\n                    print(f\'  üçé Fruit keywords found: {found_fruits}\')\n                    \n                    # Extract surrounding context for fruit mentions\n                    lines = response.text.split(\'\\n\')\n                    fruit_contexts = []\n                    \n                    for line in lines:\n                        line_lower = line.lower()\n                        if any(fruit in line_lower for fruit in found_fruits):\n                            clean_line = \' \'.join(line.split())  # Clean whitespace\n                            if len(clean_line) > 20:  # Only meaningful lines\n                                fruit_contexts.append(clean_line)\n                    \n                    if fruit_contexts:\n                        print(f\'  üìù Fruit contexts found ({len(fruit_contexts)} mentions):\')\n                        for j, context in enumerate(fruit_contexts[:5]):  # Show first 5\n                            print(f\'    {j+1}. {context[:150]}...\')\n           visual_keywords = [\'color\', \'colors\', \'light\', \'bright\', \'vibrant\', \'pattern\', \'texture\', \'embroidery\', \'textile\', \'brushstroke\']\n                found_visual = [keyword for keyword in visual_keywords if keyword in text_content]\n                \n                if found_visual:\n                    print(f\'  üé® Visual description keywords: {found_visual}\')\n            \n            accessed_sources.append({\n                \'url\': url,\n                \'status\': response.status_code,\n                \'filename\': filename,\n                \'content_type\': \'PDF\' if url.endswith(\'.pdf\') else \'HTML\',\n                \'size\': len(response.content) if url.endswith(\'.pdf\') else len(response.text),\n                \'fruits_found\': found_fruits if not url.endswith(\'.pdf\') else \'PDF_REQUIRES_EXTRACTION\'\n            })\n            \n        else:\n            print(f\'‚úó Failed to access - Status: {response.status_code}\')\n            accessed_sources.append({\n                \'url\': url,\n                \'status\': response.status_code,\n                \'error\': f\'HTTP Remove script and style elements for cleaner text analysis\n        for element in soup([\'script\', \'style\', \'nav\', \'header\', \'footer\']):\n            element.decompose()\n        \n        # Extract detailed contextual information around fruit mentions\n        fruit_contexts = []\n        lines = text_content.split(\'\\n\')\n        for line_num, line in enumerate(lines):\n            line_clean = \' \'.join(line.split()).strip()\n            if len(line_clean) > 10:  # Skip very short lines\n                line_lower = line_clean.lower()\n                \n                # Check for fruit mentions with context\n                for fruit_info in fruits_found:\n                    if fruit_info[\'term\'] in line_lower:\n                        # Get surrounding context (previous and next lines)\n                        context_start = max(0, line_num - 2)\n                        context_end = min(len(lines), line_num + 3)\n                        context_lines = lines[context_start:context_end]\n                        context = \' \'.join([\' \'.join(l.split()) for l in context_lines if l.strip()])\n                        \n                        if len(context) > 50:  # Only meaningful contexts\n                            fruit_contexts.append({\n                                \'fruit\': fruit_info[\'term\'],\n                                \'context\': context[:300] + \'...\' if len(context) > 300 else context,\n                                \'line_number\': line_num\n                            })\n        \n        if fruit_contexts:\n            print(f\'üìù Detailed fruit contexts found: {len(fruit_contexts)}\')\n            for j, ctx in enumerate(fruit_contexts[:3]):  #     "code": 'from langchain_community.document_loaders import PyPDFLoader\nimport os\nimport json\nfrom datetime import datetime\n\nprint(\'=== EXTRACTING SPECIFIC FRUITS FROM JANET FISH\\\'S "EMBROIDERY FROM UZBEKISTAN" (2008) ===\')\nprint(\'Objective: Extract and analyze specific fruits depicted with clockwise positioning details\')\nprint(\'Target: workspace/dayton_art_institute_transcript.pdf\\n\')\n\n# First, inspect the workspace to understand current file structure\nworkspace_dir = \'workspace\'\nif os.path.exists(workspace_dir):\n    workspace_files = os.listdir(workspace_dir)\n    print(f\'=== WORKSPACE INSPECTION ===\')\n    print(f\'Total files in workspace: {len(workspace_files)}\')\n    \n    # Look for PDF files\n    pdf_files = [f for f in workspace_files if f.endswith(\'.pdf\')]\n    print(f\'\\nPDF files found: {len(pdf_files)}\')\n    for pdf_file in pdf_files:\n        file_path = os.path.join(workspace_dir, pdf_file)\n        file_size = os.path.getsize(file_path)\n        print(f\'  - {pdf_file} ({file_size:,} bytes)\')\n    \n    # Check for the target PDF or find the most relevant one\n    target_pdf = \'dayton_art_institute_transcript.pdf\'\n    if target_pdf in pdf_files:\n        print(f\'\\n‚úì Target PDF found: {target_pdf}\')\n        pdf_path = os.path.join(workspace_dir, target_pdf)\n    else:\n        # Look for any Dayton-related PDF\n        dayton_pdfs = [f for f in pdf_files if \'dayton\' in f.lower()]\n        if dayton_pdfs:\n            target_pdf = dayton_pdfs[0]\n            print(f\'\\n‚úì Using Dayton PDF: {target_pdf}\')\n            pdf_path = os.path.join(workspace_dir, target_pdf)\n        else:\n            print(f\'\\n‚ùå Target PDF "{target_pdf}" not found in workspace\')\n            if pdf_files:\n                target_pdf = pdf_files[0]\n                print(f\'‚Üí Using first available PDF: {target_pdf}\')\n                pdf_path = os.path.join(workspace_dir, target_pdf)\n            else:\n                print(\'‚ùå No PDF files found in workspace\')\n                pdf_path = None\n\nelse:\n    print(\'‚ùå Workspace directory not found\')\n    pdf_path = None\n\nif pdf_path and os.path.exists(pdf_path):\n    print(f\'\\n=== EXTRACTING CONTENT FROM PDF: {target_pdf} ===\')\n    \n    try:\n        # Load and extract PDF content using LangChain\n        loader = PyPDFLoader(pdf_path)\n        pages = loader.load_and_split()\n        \n        print(f\'‚úì PDF successfully loaded\')\n        print(f\'Total pages extracted: {len(pages)}\')\n        \n        if len(pages) == 0:\n            print(\'‚ùå No pages found in PDF file\')\n        else:\n            # Combine all pages into one text\n            full_content = \'\\n\'.join([page.page_content for page in pages])\n            print(f\'Total content length: {len(full_content):,} characters\')\n            \n            # Show top 10\n                    print(f\'\\n  {i}. Parse JSON and inspect structure\n            data = json.loads(content)\n            print(f\'‚úì JSON parsed successfully - Type: {type(data).__name__}\')\n            \n            if isinstance(data, dict):\n                print(f\'Dictionary with {len(data)} top-level keys:\')\n                for key in data.keys():\n                    value = data[key]\n                    if isinstance(value, dict):\n                        print(f\'  - {key}: Dictionary with {len(value)} keys\')\n                    elif isinstance(value, list):\n                        print(f\'  - {key}: List with {len(value)} items\')\n                    else:\n                        print(f\'  - {key}: {type(value).__name__}\')\n                \n                # Extract fruit information based on discovered structure\n                file_fruit_data = {\n                    \'source_file\': target_file,\n                    \'fruits_identified\': [],\n                    \'fruit_categories\': {},\n                    \'detailed_contexts\': [],\n                    \'positioning_info\': [],\n                    \'painting_descriptions\': []\n                }\n                \n                # Look for fruit analysis section\n                if \'fruit_analysis\' in data:\n                    fruit_section = data[\'fruit_analysis\']\n                    print(f\'\\nüçé Found fruit_analysis section with {len(fruit_section)} keys\')\n                    \n                    # Extract fruits by category if available\n                    if \'fruits_by_category\' in fruit_section:\n                        fruit_categories = fruit_section[\'fruits_by_category\']\n                        file_fruit_data[\'fruit_categories\'] = fruit_categories\n                        print(f\'Fruit categories found: {list(fruit_categories.keys())}\')\n                        \n                        # Compile all unique fruits\n                        all_fruits = []\n                        for category, fruits in fruit_categories.items():\n                            all_fruits.extend(fruits)\n                        \n                        # Filter out generic terms and get unique fruits\n                        specific_fruits = []\n                        for fruit in set(all_fruits):\n                            if fruit.lower() not in [\'fruit\', \'fruits\']:  # Exclude generic terms\n                                specific_fruits.append(fruit)\n                        \n                        file_fruit_data[\'fruits_identified\'] = sorted(specific_fruits)\n                        print(f\'Specific fruits identified: {len(specific_fruits)}\')\n                    \n                    # Look for positioning analysis\n                if \'positioning_analysis\' in data:\n                    pos_section = data[\'positioning_analysis\']\n                    print(f\'\\nüìç Found positioning_analysis section\')\n                    \n                    if \'positioning_contexts\' in pos_section:\n                        positioning = pos_section[\'positioning_contexts\']\n                        file_fruit_data[\'positioning_info\'] = positioning\n                        print(f\'Positioning contexts found: {len(positioning)}\')\n                \n                # Look for painting descriptions\n                if \'painting_descriptions\' in data:\n                    desc_section = data[\'painting_descriptions\']\n                    print(f\'\\nüñºÔ∏è Found painting_descriptions section\')\n                    \n                    if \'detailed_descriptions\' in desc_section:\n                        descriptions = desc_section[\'detailed_descriptions\']\n                        file_fruit_data[\'painting_descriptions\'] = descriptions\n                        print(f\'Detailed descriptions found: {len(descriptions)}\')\n                \n                # Store data from this file\n                all_fruits_data[target_file] = file_fruit_data\n                \n        except json.JSONDecodeError as e:\n            print(f\'JSON parsing error: {str(e)}\')\n        except Exception as e:\n            print(f\'Error analyzing file: {str(e)}\')\n    \n    # Convert to singular base forms for comparison\n    if \'banana\' in fruit_lower:\n        painting_normalized.add(\'banana\')\n    elif \'lemon\' in fruit_lower:\n        painting_normalized.add(\'lemon\')\n    elif \'orange\' in fruit_lower:\n        painting_normalized.add(\'orange\')\n    elif \'peach\' in fruit_lower:\n        painting_normalized.add(\'peach\')\n    elif \'pear\' in fruit_lower:\n        painting_normalized.add(\'pear\')\n    elif \'melon\' in fruit_lower and \'watermelon\' not in fruit_lower:\n        painting_normalized.add(\'melon\')\n    elif \'watermelon\' in fruit_lower:\n        painting_normalized.add(\'watermelon\')\n    else:\n        painting_normalized.add(fruit_lower)\n\nprint(f"Painting normalized fruits: {sorted(painting_normalized)}")\n\n# Normalize ship menu fruits (extract base fruit types)\nship_normalized = set()\nfor fruit in ship_fruits:\n    fruit_lower = fruit.lower().strip()\n    # Extract base fruit types from descriptive entries\n    if \'apple\' in fruit_lower:\n        ship_normalized.add(\'apple\')\n    elif \'banana\' in fruit_lower:\n        ship_normalized.add(\'banana\')\n    elif \'orange\' in fruit_lower:\n        ship_normalized.add(\'orange\')\n    elif \'grapefruit\' in fruit_lower:\n        ship_normalized.add(\'grapefruit\')\n    elif \'grape\' in fruit_lower and \'grapefruit\' not in fruit_lower:\n        ship_normalized.add(\'grape\')\n    elif \'pear\' in fruit_lower:\n        ship_normalized.add(\'pear\')\n    elif \'peach\' in fruit_lower:\n        ship_normalized.add(\'peach\')\n    elif \'lemon\' in fruit_lower:\n        ship_normalized.add(\'lemon\')\n    elif \'pineapple\' in fruit_lower:\n        ship_normalized.add(\'pineapple\')\n    elif \'melon\' in fruit_lower:\n        ship_normalized.add(\'melon\')\n    # Convert to plural forms as requested in PLAN\n    plural_conversions = {\n        \'banana\': \'bananas\',\n        \'lemon\': \'lemons\', \n        \'orange\': \'oranges\',\n        \'peach\': \'peaches\',\n        \'pear\': \'pears\',\n        \'melon\': \'melons\',\n        \'watermelon\': \'watermelons\',\n        \'apple\': \'apples\',\n        \'grape\': \'grapes\',\n        \'grapefruit\': \'grapefruits\',\n        \'pineapple\': \'pineapples\'\n    }\n    \n    # Arrange in clockwise order based on typical still life composition\n    # Starting from 12 o\'clock and moving clockwise\n    clockwise_arrangement = []\n    \n    # Based on the fruits actually found in both sources, arrange them\n    for fruit in matching_list:\n        plural_form = plural_conversions.get(fruit, fruit + \'s\')\n        clockwise_arrangement.append(plural_form)\n    \n    print(f"\\nMatching fruits in clockwise order (plural forms):")\n    for i, fruit in enumerate(clockwise_arrangement, 1):\n        position = i * (360 / len(clockwise_arrangement))  #
